name:Dâ€aâ€wâ€aâ€wâ€a
info:Duplex Room - Courtyard-View
info:Stayed in February 2024
info:Family
info:43 Reviews
rating:4.7
posted:Posted February 24, 2024
msg:It's a pity that the hotel has a good environment design, good service, and good supplies, but the room design has big flaws. The attic room we stayed in was hot on the top and cold on the bottom due to improper installation of air conditioning and ventilation. The attic space was extremely hot, and there were no windows for ventilation and it was stuffy. We had no choice but to turn off the air conditioning and open the front and back doors to cool down and ventilate, but there was no screen door in the backyard, so mosquitoes came in at night. The private hot spring pool is very large, but the water outlet is too small. It takes about 3 hours to fill a pool of water. In addition, the location where there are steps to get into the water is blocked by the decorative partition, which is inconvenient to go up and down and there are safety hazards. It feels like a good hotel, but it's a pity that this room type has a flaw.

name:Gâ€uâ€eâ€sâ€tâ€ â€Uâ€sâ€eâ€r
info:Queen Room With Courtyard View
info:Stayed in November 2023
info:Other
info:5 Reviews
rating:5
posted:Posted November 16, 2023
msg:Last weekend, I went to see Zhang Xinzhe's concert. I originally chose Kapok, which is closer to the stadium, but later I found that there is also Dong'an Pavilion Hotel nearby.
Environment: The room looks more attractive to me. The whole hotel is designed in Chinese style, with very careful garden landscape.
Transportation: You can choose to take a sightseeing bus or walk from the hotel to the venue. The sightseeing bus costs 10 yuan per person, and it takes about 20 minutes to walk.
Facilities: It rained and the temperature dropped that day. It was very comfortable to take a bath in the room after watching the concert. Remember to bring a disposable bath bag. The hotel provides bath salts.
Service: Front desk, room service, restaurant, everyone's service attitude is very good.
Breakfast: The only thing I am not satisfied with is that the breakfast variety and taste are average.
